*Francis Kulumba,Wissam Antoun,Théo Lasnier,Benoît Sagot,Djamé Seddah*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文首次识别了8B参数自回归语言模型中语言切换后门攻击的完整神经回路，揭示了三阶段机制：早期注意力头组合触发词、中间层在正交子空间传播信号、最终层MLP转换为目标语言logits，并发现该攻击通过单个位置的串行瓶颈实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 后门攻击对语言模型构成日益增长的安全威胁，但触发序列如何劫持模型计算的内部机制仍缺乏理解。

Method: 通过电路分析，将语言切换后门分解为三个阶段：(1)早期分布注意力头将9个触发token组合到最后一个序列位置；(2)中间层在正交于自然语言方向子空间传播信号；(3)最终层MLP将潜在信号转换为法语logits。并验证了单个位置串行瓶颈的关键作用。

Result: 发现整个电路通过单个位置的串行瓶颈流动；破坏该位置可完全消除触发但损害模型能力；正交潜在编码使得基于中间表征语言信号的防御方法无效。

Conclusion: 该后门利用正交子空间逃避检测，揭示了现有防御机制的盲区，为开发更鲁棒的后门防御提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Backdoor attacks on language models pose a growing security concern, yet the internal mechanisms by which a trigger sequence hijacks model computations remain poorly understood. We identify a circuit underlying a language-switching backdoor in an 8B-parameter autoregressive language model, where a three-word Latin trigger (nine tokens) redirects English output to French. We decompose the circuit into three phases: (1) distributed attention heads at early layers compose the trigger tokens into the last sequence position; (2) the resulting signal propagates through mid-layers in a subspace orthogonal to the model's natural language-identity direction; (3) the MLP at the final layer converts this latent signal into French logits. The entire circuit flows through a serial bottleneck at a single position: corrupting that position at any layer entirely mitigate the trigger but also hinder the model's capabilities. The orthogonal latent encoding suggests that defenses that search for language-like signals in intermediate representations would miss this trigger entirely.

</details>


### [345] [EnvFactory: Scaling Tool-Use Agents via Executable Environments Synthesis and Robust RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18703)
*Minrui Xu,Zilin Wang,Mengyi DENG,Zhiwei Li,Zhicheng Yang,Xiao Zhu,Yinhong Liu,Boyu Zhu,Baiyu Huang,Chao Chen,Heyuan Deng,Fei Mi,Lifeng Shang,Xingshan Zeng,Zhijiang Guo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: EnvFactory是一个全自动框架，通过从真实资源中自主构建可执行的工具环境，并合成自然的、包含隐式意图的多轮轨迹，解决了LLM工具使用中环境可扩展性和训练数据稀缺两大瓶颈，仅用85个环境就显著提升了模型在多个基准上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于Agentic RL的LLM工具使用训练面临两大挑战：缺乏可扩展且稳健的执行环境，以及缺乏能够捕捉人类隐式推理的真实训练数据。现有方法依赖昂贵的真实API、易产生幻觉的LLM模拟器或合成环境，且合成轨迹往往过度明确，类似指令序列而非自然的人类意图，降低了RL训练的有效性。

Method: EnvFactory采用全自动框架，首先从真实资源自主探索和验证有状态、可执行的工具环境，然后通过拓扑感知采样和校准优化合成自然的、包含隐式意图的多轮轨迹。仅使用85个经过验证的环境（覆盖7个领域），生成了2,575条SFT和RL轨迹。

Result: 相比先前工作需要多达5倍的环境数量，EnvFactory实现了更优的训练效率和下游性能：在BFCLv3上提升+15%，在MCP-Atlas上提升+8.6%，在τ²-Bench和VitaBench等对话基准上提升+6%。

Conclusion: EnvFactory通过完全自动化环境构建和轨迹合成，为Agentic RL提供了可扩展、可扩展且稳健的基础，有效解决了数据稀缺和环境构建的两大瓶颈。

Abstract: Equipping LLMs with tool-use capabilities via Agentic Reinforcement Learning (Agentic RL) is bottlenecked by two challenges: the lack of scalable, robust execution environments and the scarcity of realistic training data that captures implicit human reasoning. Existing approaches depend on costly real-world APIs, hallucination-prone LLM simulators, or synthetic environments that are often single-turn or depend on pre-collected documents. Moreover, synthetic trajectories are frequently over-specified, resembling instruction sequences rather than natural human intents, reducing their effectiveness for RL training. We introduce EnvFactory, a fully automated framework that addresses both challenges. EnvFactory autonomously explores and verifies stateful, executable tool environments from authentic resources, and synthesizes natural multi-turn trajectories through topology-aware sampling and calibrated refinement, producing grounded queries with implicit intents. Using only 85 verified environments across 7 domains, EnvFactory generates 2,575 SFT and RL trajectories. Despite using significantly fewer environments than prior work, which are often 5 times more, EnvFactory achieves superior training efficiency and downstream performance, improving Qwen3-series models by up to +15% on BFCLv3, +8.6% on MCP-Atlas, and +6% on conversational benchmarks including $τ^2$-Bench and VitaBench. By fully automating both environment construction and trajectory synthesis, EnvFactory provides a scalable, extensible, and robust foundation for Agentic RL.

</details>


### [346] [Predictable Confabulations: Factual Recall by LLMs Scales with Model Size and Topic Frequency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18732)
*Matthew L. Smith,Jonathan P. Shock,Samuel T. Segun,Iyiola E. Olatunji,Tegawendé F. Bissyandé*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究发现，模型的事实召回能力遵循S形曲线，该曲线由模型参数量与训练数据中主题表征的对数线性组合决定。这两个变量单独能解释16个稠密模型60%的方差，在单个模型家族内可达到74-94%。这一现象符合叠加理论的解释：召回能力由信噪比门控，信号强度随概念频率增长，噪声基底随模型容量增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管缩放定律已经能够预测大型语言模型的整体性能表现，但尚未有缩放定律将事实召回能力与模型规模及训练数据构成联系起来。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 在38个模型上使用自动引用验证系统评估了超过8,900条学术参考文献的召回质量，并分析了模型参数量与训练数据中主题表征对召回表现的影响。

Result: 召回质量遵循参数量与训练数据表征对数线性组合的S形曲线。这两个变量解释了16个稠密模型60%的方差，在单个模型家族内提升至74-94%。

Conclusion: 这一结果与叠加理论的解释一致——事实召回由信噪比门控，信号强度与概念在训练数据中的频率成正比，噪声基底与模型容量成正比。

Abstract: While scaling laws govern aggregate large language model performance, no scaling law has linked factual recall to both model size and training-data composition. We evaluated 38 models on over 8,900 scholarly references evaluated by an automated reference verification system. Recall quality follows a sigmoid in the log-linear combination of model parameter count and topic representation in training data. These two variables alone explain 60% of the variance across 16 dense models from four families, rising to 74-94% within individual families. The form matches a superposition-inspired account in which recall is gated by a signal-to-noise ratio: signal strength scales with concept frequency and the noise floor with model capacity.

</details>


### [347] [Code as Agent Harness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18747)
*Xuying Ning,Katherine Tieu,Dongqi Fu,Tianxin Wei,Zihao Li,Yuanchen Bei,Jiaru Zou,Mengting Ai,Zhining Liu,Ting-Wei Li,Lingjie Chen,Yanjun Zhao,Ke Yang,Bingxuan Li,Cheng Qian,Gaotang Li,Xiao Lin,Zhichen Zeng,Ruizhong Qiu,Sirui Chen,Yifan Sun,Xiyuan Yang,Ruida Wang,Rui Pan,Chenyuan Yang,Dylan Zhang,Liri Fang,Zikun Cui,Yang Cao,Pan Chen,Dorothy Sun,Ren Chen,Mahesh Srinivasan,Nipun Mathur,Yinglong Xia,Hong Li,Hong Yan,Pan Lu,Lingming Zhang,Tong Zhang,Hanghang Tong,Jingrui He*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出"代码作为智能体框架"的统一视角，系统梳理了代码在智能体系统中的三重作用：作为连接推理、行动与环境建模的接口，作为规划、记忆与工具使用的机制支撑，以及作为多智能体协作与验证的共享基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在代码理解和生成方面展现出强大能力，代码不再仅仅是目标输出，而是日益成为智能体推理、行动、环境建模和执行验证的操作基础。现有研究分散在不同方向，缺乏统一视角来系统理解这一转变。

Method: 围绕三个层次组织综述：(1)框架接口层——代码连接智能体与推理、行动和环境建模；(2)框架机制层——规划、记忆、工具使用及反馈驱动的控制与优化；(3)框架扩展层——从单智能体到多智能体系统的共享代码工件协调与验证。

Result: 总结了代码作为智能体框架的代表性方法和实际应用，涵盖编码助手、GUI/OS自动化、具身智能体、科学发现、个性化推荐、DevOps和企业工作流等领域。

Conclusion: 提出以代码为中心的统一路线图，构建可执行、可验证、有状态的AI智能体系统，并指出评估超越最终任务成功、不完全反馈下的验证、无回归改进、多智能体状态共享、安全关键行动的人类监督及多模态环境扩展等开放挑战。

Abstract: Recent large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong capabilities in understanding and generating code, from competitive programming to repository-level software engineering. In emerging agentic systems, code is no longer only a target output. It increasingly serves as an operational substrate for agent reasoning, acting, environment modeling, and execution-based verification. We frame this shift through the lens of agent harnesses and introduce code as agent harness: a unified view that centers code as the basis for agent infrastructure. To systematically study this perspective, we organize the survey around three connected layers. First, we study the harness interface, where code connects agents to reasoning, action, and environment modeling. Second, we examine harness mechanisms: planning, memory, and tool use for long-horizon execution, together with feedback-driven control and optimization that make harness reliable and adaptive. Third, we discuss scaling the harness from single-agent systems to multi-agent settings, where shared code artifacts support multi-agent coordination, review, and verification. Across these layers, we summarize representative methods and practical applications of code as agent harness, spanning coding assistants, GUI/OS automation, embodied agents, scientific discovery, personalization and recommendation, DevOps, and enterprise workflows. We further outline open challenges for harness engineering, including evaluation beyond final task success, verification under incomplete feedback, regression-free harness improvement, consistent shared state across multiple agents, human oversight for safety-critical actions, and extensions to multimodal environments. By centering code as the harness of agentic AI, this survey provides a unified roadmap toward executable, verifiable, and stateful AI agent systems.

</details>


### [348] [DashAttention: Differentiable and Adaptive Sparse Hierarchical Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18753)
*Yuxiang Huang,Nuno M. T. Gonçalves,Federico Alvetreti,Lei Li,Xu Han,Edoardo M. Ponti,André F. T. Martins,Marcos V. Treviso*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: DashAttention提出一种可微分且自适应的稀疏分层注意力机制，使用α-entmax变换替代固定top-k操作，实现变长块选择，保持端到端可微性，在75%稀疏度下达到与全注意力相当的准确率，并优于NSA和InfLLMv2。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分层注意力方法（如NSA、InfLLMv2）使用固定top-k选择块，假设每个查询的相关token数量固定，且阻断稀疏与密集阶段之间的梯度流动，限制了模型的灵活性和训练效果。

Method: 提出DashAttention，第一阶段使用自适应稀疏的α-entmax变换选择可变数量的相关块，为第二阶段的softmax注意力提供先验，使整个层级结构保持可微分。

Result: 在LLM上达到75%稀疏度下与全注意力相当的准确率；相比NSA和InfLLMv2，在高稀疏度场景下取得更优的Pareto前沿；基于Triton的高效实现在推理时速度超过FlashAttention-3。

Conclusion: DashAttention是一种经济高效的长上下文建模策略，通过可微分层稀疏注意力在保持精度的同时实现显著加速。

Abstract: Current hierarchical attention methods, such as NSA and InfLLMv2, select the top-k relevant key-value (KV) blocks based on coarse attention scores and subsequently apply fine-grained softmax attention on the selected tokens. However, the top-k operation assumes the number of relevant tokens for any query is fixed and it precludes the gradient flow between the sparse and dense stages. In this work, we propose DashAttention (Differentiable and Adaptive Sparse Hierarchical Attention), which leverages the adaptively sparse $α$-entmax transformation to select a variable number of blocks according to the current query in the first stage. This in turn provides a prior for the second-stage softmax attention, keeping the entire hierarchy fully differentiable. Contrary to other hierarchical attention methods, we show that DashAttention is non-dispersive, translating to better long-context modeling ability. Experiments with large language models (LLMs) show that DashAttention achieves comparable accuracy as full attention with 75% sparsity and a better Pareto frontier than NSA and InfLLMv2, especially in high-sparsity regimes. We also provide an efficient, GPU-aware implementation of DashAttention in Triton, which achieves a speedup of up to over FlashAttention-3 at inference time. Overall, DashAttention offers a cost-effective strategy to model long contexts.

</details>
